<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tram">Tram</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Tram">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Moscow_trammap.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1132" data-file-width="1000" height="249" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Moscow_trammap.png/220px-Moscow_trammap.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Moscow_trammap.png/330px-Moscow_trammap.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Moscow_trammap.png/440px-Moscow_trammap.png 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Moscow_trammap.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Trams_in_Moscow" title="Trams in Moscow">Moscow Tram Network</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image">
<div style="width:52px"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg"><img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/></a></div>
</td>
<td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>. <span class="hide-when-compact">Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span> <small><i>(April 2014)</i></small> <small class="hide-when-compact"><i>(<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>Moscow has an extensive tram system, which first opened in 1899. The newest line was built in 1984. Its daily usage by Muscovites is low, making up for approximately 5% of trips, because many vital connections in the network have been withdrawn. Trams still remain important in some districts as feeders to Metro stations. The trams also provide important cross links between metro lines, for example between <a href="/wiki/Universitet_(Moscow_Metro)" title="Universitet (Moscow Metro)">Universitet station</a> of <a href="/wiki/Sokolnicheskaya_Line" title="Sokolnicheskaya Line">Sokolnicheskaya Line</a> (#1 red line) and <a href="/wiki/Profsoyuznaya_(Moscow_Metro)" title="Profsoyuznaya (Moscow Metro)">Profsoyuznaya station</a> of <a href="/wiki/Kaluzhsko-Rizhskaya_Line" title="Kaluzhsko-Rizhskaya Line">Kaluzhsko-Rizhskaya Line</a> (#6 orange line) or between <a href="/wiki/Voykovskaya_(Moscow_Metro)" title="Voykovskaya (Moscow Metro)">Voykovskaya</a> and <a href="/wiki/Strogino_(Moscow_Metro)" title="Strogino (Moscow Metro)">Strogino</a>.</p>
<p>There are three tram networks in the city:</p>
<ul>
<li>Krasnopresnenskoye depot network with the westernmost point at Strogino (depot location) and the easternmost point near platform Dmitrovskaya. This network became separated in 1973, but until 1997 it could easily have been reconnected by about one kilometre (0.62 miles) of track and three switches. The network has the highest usage in Moscow and no weak points based on turnover except to-depot lane (passengers serviced by bus) and tram ring at Dmitrovskaya (because now it is neither a normal transfer point nor a repair terminal).</li>
<li>The Apakov depot services the south-western part from the Varshavsky lane – Simferopolsky boulevard in the east to the Universitet station in the west and Boulevard lane at the center. This network is connected only by the four-way Dubininskaya and Kozhevnicheskaya streets. A second connection by Vostochnaya (Eastern) street was withdrawn in 1987 due to fire at Dinamo plant and has not been recovered, and remains lost (Avtozavodsky bridge) at 1992. The network may be serviced anyway by another depot (now route 35, 38).</li>
<li>Main three depot networks with railway gate and tram-repair plant.</li>
</ul>
<p>In addition, tram advocates have suggested that the new rapid transit services (metro to City, Butovo light metro, Monorail) would be more effective as at-grade tram lines and that the current problems with trams are only due to poor management and operation, not the technical properties of trams. New tram models have been developed for the Moscow network despite the lack of expansion.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Taxi">Taxi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Taxi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Taxi service market in Moscow has changed dramatically over the years 2014–2015. New technology and service platforms <a class="external text" href="https://taxi.yandex.ru/" rel="nofollow">Yandex.Taxi</a>, <a class="external text" href="https://www.uber.com/" rel="nofollow">Uber</a> and <a class="external text" href="http://gett.com/ru/" rel="nofollow">Gett</a> (ex-GetTaxi) displaced many private drivers and small service providers. By the beginning of 2015 newcomers were servicing more than 50% of all taxi orders in Moscow and are still rapidly growing.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147"><a href="#cite_note-147">[147]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup><br/>
A taxi can be called using a smartphone, tablet or PC in 5–15 minutes. Commercial taxi services are available. In addition, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Route_taxi" title="Route taxi">route taxis</a> are in widespread use.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Roads">Roads</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Roads">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:High_traffic.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2448" data-file-width="3264" height="173" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/High_traffic.jpg/230px-High_traffic.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/High_traffic.jpg/345px-High_traffic.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/High_traffic.jpg/460px-High_traffic.jpg 2x" width="230"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:High_traffic.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Traffic congestion</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>There are over 2.6 million cars in the city daily. Recent years have seen the growth in the number of cars, which have caused traffic jams and lack of parking space to become major problems.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Moscow_Ring_Road" title="Moscow Ring Road">MKAD</a>, along with the <a href="/wiki/Third_Ring_Road_(Moscow)" title="Third Ring Road (Moscow)">Third Transport Ring</a> and the future Fourth Transport Ring, is one of only three freeways that run within Moscow city limits. There are several other roadway systems that form <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Concentric_circles" title="Concentric circles">concentric circles</a> around the city.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Future_development">Future development</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Future development">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Moscow-City2015.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="683" data-file-width="1024" height="267" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Moscow-City2015.jpg/400px-Moscow-City2015.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Moscow-City2015.jpg/600px-Moscow-City2015.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Moscow-City2015.jpg/800px-Moscow-City2015.jpg 2x" width="400"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Moscow-City2015.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Moscow_International_Business_Center" title="Moscow International Business Center">Moscow International Business Center</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Moscow_International_Business_Center" title="Moscow International Business Center">Moscow International Business Center</a> is a projected new part of central Moscow. Situated in <a href="/wiki/Presnensky_District" title="Presnensky District">Presnensky District</a>, located at the <a href="/wiki/Third_Ring_Road_(Moscow)" title="Third Ring Road (Moscow)">Third Ring</a>, the Moscow City area is under intense development. The goal of <a href="/wiki/Moscow_International_Business_Center" title="Moscow International Business Center">MIBC</a> is to create a zone, the first in Russia, and in all of Eastern Europe,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup> that will combine business activity, living space and entertainment. The project was conceived by the Moscow government in 1992.</p>
<p>The construction of <a href="/wiki/Moscow_International_Business_Center" title="Moscow International Business Center">Moscow-City</a> takes place on the Krasnopresnenskaya embankment. The whole project takes up to one square kilometre (250 acres). The area is the only spot in downtown Moscow that can accommodate a project of this magnitude. Today, most of the buildings there are old factories and industrial complexes.</p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Federation_Tower" title="Federation Tower">Federation Tower</a>, completed in 2016, is the tallest building in Europe. Also to be included in the project are a <a href="/wiki/Water_park" title="Water park">water park</a> and other recreational facilities; business and entertainment complexes, office and residential buildings, the transport network and the <a href="/wiki/City_Hall_and_City_Duma" title="City Hall and City Duma">new site of the Moscow government</a>. The construction of four new metro stations in the territory has been completed, two of which have opened and two others are reserved for future metro lines crossing <a href="/wiki/Moscow_International_Business_Center" title="Moscow International Business Center">MIBC</a>, some additional stations were planned. A rail shuttle service, directly connecting <a href="/wiki/Moscow_International_Business_Center" title="Moscow International Business Center">MIBC</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Sheremetyevo_International_Airport" title="Sheremetyevo International Airport">Sheremetyevo International Airport</a> is also planned. Major thoroughfares through <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moscow-City" title="Moscow-City">Moscow-City</a> are the <a href="/wiki/Third_Ring_Road_(Moscow)" title="Third Ring Road (Moscow)">Third Ring</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kutuzovsky_Prospekt" title="Kutuzovsky Prospekt">Kutuzovsky Prospekt</a>. Three metro stations were initially planned for the <a href="/wiki/Filyovskaya_Line" title="Filyovskaya Line">Filyovskaya Line</a>. The station Delovoi Tsentr opened in 2005, and was later renamed <a href="/wiki/Vystavochnaya" title="Vystavochnaya">Vystavochnaya</a> in 2009. The branch extended to the <a href="/wiki/Mezhdunarodnaya_(Moscow_Metro)" title="Mezhdunarodnaya (Moscow Metro)">Mezhdunarodnaya</a> station in 2006, and all work on third station, Dorogomilovskaya (between <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kiyevskaya_(Filyovskaya)" title="Kiyevskaya (Filyovskaya)">Kiyevskaya</a> and Delovoi Tsentr), has been postponed. There are plans to extend the branch as far as the <a href="/wiki/Savyolovskaya" title="Savyolovskaya">Savyolovskaya</a> station, on the <a href="/wiki/Serpukhovsko-Timiryazevskaya_Line" title="Serpukhovsko-Timiryazevskaya Line">Serpukhovsko-Timiryazevskaya Line</a>.</p>
<p>A Fourth Ring freeway (in addition to Moscow Automobile Ring Road, <a href="/wiki/Garden_Ring" title="Garden Ring">Garden Ring</a> and the Third Ring) has been designed and is being built around Moscow. It is to be completed by 2012 and will have a total length of 61 kilometres (38 mi).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup></p>
<p>A rail connection linking the international airports at Vnukovo and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sheremetyevo_Airport" title="Sheremetyevo Airport">Sheremetyevo</a> with downtown terminals is also planned.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>In March 2009 the Russian business newspaper <i>Kommersant</i><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup> reported that because of the worldwide economic crisis, which started in 2008 and spread globally, many of the construction projects in Moscow (especially in the <a href="/wiki/Moscow_International_Business_Center" title="Moscow International Business Center">Moscow International Business Center</a>) are frozen and may be cancelled altogether—like the ambitious "Russia Tower" in "Moscow-city".</p>
<ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">
<li class="gallerycaption">Skyscrapers in Moscow International Business Center</li>
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 62px">
<div style="width: 62px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 60px;">
<div style="margin:0px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:OKO_Towers2016.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="1041" data-file-width="520" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/OKO_Towers2016.jpg/90px-OKO_Towers2016.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/OKO_Towers2016.jpg/135px-OKO_Towers2016.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/OKO_Towers2016.jpg/180px-OKO_Towers2016.jpg 2x" width="60"/></a></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media">Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/Media_of_Russia" title="Media of Russia">Media of Russia</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Headquartered_RIA_Novosti_01.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="683" data-file-width="1024" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Headquartered_RIA_Novosti_01.png/220px-Headquartered_RIA_Novosti_01.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Headquartered_RIA_Novosti_01.png/330px-Headquartered_RIA_Novosti_01.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Headquartered_RIA_Novosti_01.png/440px-Headquartered_RIA_Novosti_01.png 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Headquartered_RIA_Novosti_01.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/RIA_Novosti" title="RIA Novosti">RIA Novosti</a> headquarters in Moscow</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Moscow is home to nearly all of Russia's nationwide <a href="/wiki/Television_in_Russia" title="Television in Russia">television networks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Radio_station" title="Radio station">radio stations</a>, newspapers and magazines.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Newspapers">Newspapers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Newspapers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Further information: <a href="/wiki/List_of_newspapers_in_Russia" title="List of newspapers in Russia">List of newspapers in Russia</a></div>
<p>English-language media include <i><a href="/wiki/The_Moscow_Times" title="The Moscow Times">The Moscow Times</a></i> and <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moscow_News" title="Moscow News">Moscow News</a></i>, which are, respectively, the largest<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup> and oldest English-language weekly newspapers in all of Russia. <i><a href="/wiki/Kommersant" title="Kommersant">Kommersant</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Vedomosti" title="Vedomosti">Vedomosti</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Novaya_Gazeta" title="Novaya Gazeta">Novaya Gazeta</a></i> are Russian-language media headquartered in Moscow. <i>Kommersant</i> and <i>Vedomosti</i> are among the country's leading and oldest Russian-language business newspapers.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="TV_and_radio">TV and radio</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: TV and radio">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/Television_in_Russia" title="Television in Russia">Television in Russia</a> and <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Radio_in_Russia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Radio in Russia (page does not exist)">Radio in Russia</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">

<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:%D0%A2%D0%B5%D0%BB%D0%B5%D1%86%D0%B5%D0%BD%D1%82%D1%80_%D0%9E%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE_(04.01.2014)_7.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Ostankino_Technical_Center" title="Ostankino Technical Center">Ostankino Technical Center</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:View_from_Imperia_Tower_Moscow_04-2014_img04.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2419" data-file-width="3629" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/View_from_Imperia_Tower_Moscow_04-2014_img04.jpg/220px-View_from_Imperia_Tower_Moscow_04-2014_img04.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/View_from_Imperia_Tower_Moscow_04-2014_img04.jpg/330px-View_from_Imperia_Tower_Moscow_04-2014_img04.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/View_from_Imperia_Tower_Moscow_04-2014_img04.jpg/440px-View_from_Imperia_Tower_Moscow_04-2014_img04.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>

</div>
</div>
<p>Other media in Moscow include the <i><a href="/wiki/Echo_of_Moscow" title="Echo of Moscow">Echo of Moscow</a></i>, the first Soviet and Russian private news radio and information agency, and <a href="/wiki/NTV_(Russia)" title="NTV (Russia)">NTV</a>, one of the first privately owned Russian television stations. The total number of radio stations in Moscow in the FM band is near 50.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Famous_people">Famous people</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Famous people">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Category:People_from_Moscow" title="Category:People from Moscow">Category:People from Moscow</a></div>

<p>Some of the notable people are <a href="/wiki/Boris_Pasternak" title="Boris Pasternak">Boris Pasternak</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fyodor_Dostoyevsky" title="Fyodor Dostoyevsky">Fyodor Dostoyevsky</a> (writers), and <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Brin" title="Sergey Brin">Sergey Brin</a>, (co-founder of Google).</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cooperation_agreements">Cooperation agreements</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Cooperation agreements">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Moscow has cooperation agreements with:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal"><img alt="Portugal" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="600" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/23px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/35px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/45px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Lisbon" title="Lisbon">Lisbon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lisbon_twinnings_183-0"><a href="#cite_note-Lisbon_twinnings-183">[183]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lisbon_twinnings_2_184-0"><a href="#cite_note-Lisbon_twinnings_2-184">[184]</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran"><img alt="Iran" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="360" data-file-width="630" height="13" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Flag_of_Iran.svg/23px-Flag_of_Iran.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Flag_of_Iran.svg/35px-Flag_of_Iran.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Flag_of_Iran.svg/46px-Flag_of_Iran.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands"><img alt="Netherlands" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">The Netherlands</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Former_twin_towns_and_sister_cities">Former twin towns and sister cities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Former twin towns and sister cities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine"><img alt="Ukraine" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="1200" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Flag_of_Ukraine.svg/23px-Flag_of_Ukraine.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Flag_of_Ukraine.svg/35px-Flag_of_Ukraine.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/Flag_of_Ukraine.svg/45px-Flag_of_Ukraine.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Kiev" title="Kiev">Kiev</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185"><a href="#cite_note-185">[185]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rankings">Rankings</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Moscow&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Rankings">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The international rankings of Moscow are:</p>
<ul>
<li>The most populous city in Russia, and the most populous city entirely in Europe</li>
<li>The most populated inland city</li>
<li>World's northernmost megacity</li>
<li>City with the largest trolleybus system in the world</li>
<li>Major city with the most forest within its borders</li>
<li>City with the busiest subway system in Europe, and the third busiest worldwide</li>
<li>City with the highest building in Europe (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mercury_Tower" title="Mercury Tower">Mercury Tower</a>)</li>
<li>City with the highest structure in Europe (<a href="/wiki/Ostankino_Tower" title="Ostankino Tower">Ostankino Tower</a>)</li>
</ul>

<td class="navbox-list navbox-odd plainlist" colspan="2" style="width:100%;padding:0px;background:transparent;color:inherit;">
<div style="padding:0px;">
<table class="navbox-columns-table" style="border-spacing: 0px; text-align:left;width:100%;">
<tr style="vertical-align:top;">
<td style="padding:0px;text-align:left; padding-left:0.2em; white-space:nowrap;;;;width:10em;">
<div>
<ul>
